1/12/21, 12:19â€¯PM - Sainath IIITNR: I think there s a lot of misunderstanding about privacy and security thatâ€™s been articulated in many groups and especially on social media, as someone who is very particular about devices and accounts being secure let me dispel some of the myths, Whatsapp collects data, and a few days ago I posted a link here that shows what data Whatsapp collects about each individual, there is nothing new in that, Whatsapp has always been doing that from the beginning, Whatsapp has info on your phone number, other people s phone numbers in your contacts, your status updates and when you were last online. Since 2016 Whatsapp has been sharing that data with its parent company, Facebook. Whatsapp however has an option where an user can opt out of sharing the data with Facebook, how many in this group have ever exercised that option? I donâ€™t think a single person here has exercised that option, now the only thing that has changed is -that option wonâ€™t be available anymore,  so post February 8th Whatsapp will be sharing everyoneâ€™s data with Facebook, which is already the case with most people, except the people who have exercised the option of not sharing their WA data with Facebook, that option wonâ€™t exist anymore. So technically nothing will change, your info is already shared with Facebook since 2016 and that will continue. The reason that Whatsapp is doing this is because Facebook wants to monetise their investments by targeted advertising and Facebook is doing this because phone manufacturers , especially Apple, are addressing privacy concerns and with Apple s iOS 14 update, Users have to give consent to being tracked by Facebook. So for people who are troubled by this there are other options like Telegram and Signal, Telegram is a Russian app and itâ€™s management is shrouded in secrecy, they keep changing their operational headquarters and Telegram like Whatsapp is not an altruistic venture and they too want to monetise their investments and they are also building a platform for targeted advertising, and also Telegram is not completely end to end encrypted and they store all user data with their decryption keys on their servers and Telegram has been hacked many times and most famously in Iran, where data about millions of accounts were stolen. That leaves only Signal, Signal was founded by Brian Acton, one of the creators and founders of Whatsapp, after he sold Whatsapp to Facebook. Signal is end to end encrypted and doesnâ€™t collect much data except your phone number.. and your data is not saved on servers but your device. Signal is run by a non profit organisation and doesnâ€™t want to monetise their investments and is run by â€˜donationsâ€™, because Signals working model is altruistic and their funding is based on donations only, I seriously doubt that they can scale up to manage much more  than the users they already have, running a messaging app requires lot of investments in technology, especially big servers , Signal has about 40 million users now, and if more migrate there rapidly, their systems will crash and it has already happened and I donâ€™t know how a non profit messaging app can survive catering to hundreds of millions or a Billion users. Also since Signal s data is not stored on on a Server/Cloud but locally on your device, so every time you buy a new phone  you will have to manually transfer your old Signal messages and data, and there is nothing much you can do if your phone crashes.

2/3/21, 11:34â€¯AM - +91 86026 16019: Interview session can be an open-ended session since we can instantly ask questions from the answers that they have given.

Certain phrases should be used so that session goes smoothly.

Body language should be maintained during interview because depending on the signals of non verbal questions you will get sementic responses.

Record the session so that we can analyse body language and write the transcript.

Speaking and listening should get hand in hand,they are the most important skills.

You can encourage the speaker by using certain phrases.

You should acknowledge the speaker.

You should immediately ask question if you have any doubt.

4/7/21, 6:57â€¯PM - +91 73930 40493: Dear Students,

End Term Examination has been scheduled. It will be a multiple-choice questions & answer.

 

Details of the End Term Examination are given below:

Subject:  Digital Logic Design (EC101C)

Branch: 1-SEM; ECE, CSE, DSAI (B.Tech); Autumn-2020 Semester;

Date: 16.04.2021;

Starting time: 11.0 am;

Duration: 40 minutes.

Max Marks: 50 (1 mark is awarded for each correct answer while 1/4 mark is deducted for every wrong answer).

Instructor Code: MA;

The link of google form for Multiple Choice Questions & Answers will be given few minutes before the exam start.

 

Submit it within 11.40 am. If you submit it after 11.40 am, your obtained marks will be reduced by 1.0 per 60 seconds of late submission.

The link will be deactivated at 1.0 pm on 16th April 2021.

Please try to complete it on time.

NB: You can fill out this form only once.

 

 

 

Modules / Topics will be covered in this exam:

1)      Number system and Logic Gates: Binary number system, Octal, Hexa decimal, base conversions, signed and unsigned numbers, complements, addition, subtraction using complements, Different Binary codes, operation, Truth tables of different logic gates.

2)      Boolean Algebra and K-maps: Basic Theorems and postulates, properties of Boolean algebra, Boolean functions, standard and canonical forms, 2,3,4- variable K-map methods of simplification, NAND/NOR implementations, other two level implementations, Multi-level implementations, 2-3 variable XOR function, Logic Simplification using Tabular method, etc.

3)      Combinational Circuit Design: Design procedure, Different Adders and Subtractors-Half Adder, Full Adder, Half Subtractor, Full Subtractor, 4-bit Ripple Carry Adder, Carry Look Ahead Adder, Decoder, Encoders, Multiplexers, De-Multiplexers, Magnitude Comparator, etc.

4)      Sequential Circuit Design: Basics, Latches and Flip-flops, conversion from one FF to another, Designing of serial and Parallel Registers, Synchronous and Asynchronous Counter Designing, Mealy and Moore Machine.


NB: If you have any questions regarding this MCQ end term exam, please feel free to discuss with me through mobile phone, email, or WhatsApp.


--
Sincerely,
**************************************************************************
Dr. Maifuz Ali
Assistant Professor

Electronics & Communication Engineering (ECE)

Despite having no formal education in pure mathematics, he made significant contributions to Mathematical Analysis, number theory, infinite series and the list goes on.

*Mathematica is open to all Quiz*

Participants shall be shortlisted based on accuracy and time taken to answer each question.

Round 2 being a live buzzer session will be held on Google Meet.

4/17/22, 1:40â€¯PM - +91 88899 30610: DAA Syllabus: 
1) Time and Space Complexity Analysis: Best, Worst and Average Time and Space Complexity
2) Solving Recurrence Relations: Master's Theorem, Substitution and Tree Method 
3) Searching Algorithms: Linear and Binary Search(DnC)
4) Sorting Algorithms: Merge Sort(DnC), Quick Sort(DnC), Insertion Sort, Heap Sort, and Hybrid Sort
5) Greedy Problems: Fractional Knapsack(Sorting), Huffman Coding(Heap), Job Sequencing with Deadlines(Sorting), Optimal Merge Pattern(Heap) and Strassens Matrix Multiplication(DnC)
6) Minimum Spanning Tree Algorithms: Prims(heap), and Kruskals(DSU and sorting) [Basics of graphs discussed in the class i.e. kirchhoff theorem for graphs, no. of edges in a tree, what is a graph]

â€œIt is better to debate a question without settling it than to settle a question without debating it."
â€• Joseph Joubert                                                                                                                                               
 
Cover to Cover, in collaboration with Take da Bait, is hosting the event 'DISCEPTATIO', a debate competition where you will get a chance to put your thoughts forward and make your voice heard on the topic:

Brain Drain: Is the International migration of Indian youth worth justifying?

It is common for students to leave immediately after finishing their studies at any of our country's prestigious institutions. A significant portion of the money invested in these bright minds benefits corporations in first-world countries. However, the remuneration they receive in our country for their skills is insufficient. Is it a good idea to get into one of the best colleges in the country, finish your degree, and then use your degree to make money for others?

The details of the competition are as follows:
Date: 13th January 2022
Time: 6:30 Onwards
Platform: Google Meet
Rules are in the given doc - https://docs.google.com/document/d/1EBUKrJkNgcrZbu7P1hzfZdJmDow8y9qVlc_rSwmJ9Nw/edit

Entries will be considered till 2:00 PM, 13th January 2022

-Nita Ambani

Looking forward to the prompt responses!!
Have a pleasant day ahead!
